The implementation includes two distinct patterns: the classic group coordination protocol and the modern (KIP-848) group coordination protocol.\\n\\n## Classic Group State Machine\\n\\nThe classic protocol is defined in the following files:\\n\\n1. **ClassicGroupState.java** - Defines an enum with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: Group has no members, waiting for joins\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE: Group is initiating a rebalance, collecting join requests\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE: Group awaits state assignment from leader\\n   - STABLE: Group is stable with members assigned\\n   - DEAD: Group is being deleted\\n\\n   The state enum includes validPreviousStates() method defining valid transitions:\\n   - EMPTY -> PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n   - PREPARING_REBALANCE -> EMPTY or COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n   - COMPLETING_REBALANCE -> STABLE\\n   - STABLE -> PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n\\n2. **ClassicGroup.java** - Implements the group state machine with:\\n   - transitionTo(ClassicGroupState) method for state transitions\\n   - assertValidTransition() to enforce valid state changes\\n   - canRebalance() to check if group can enter rebalance\\n\\n3. **ClassicGroupMember.java** - Represents individual members in classic groups\\n\\n## Modern Consumer Group State Machine\\n\\nThe modern protocol (introduced in KIP-848) is implemented in:\\n\\n1. **ConsumerGroup.java** - Defines ConsumerGroupState enum with five states:\\n   - EMPTY: No members in group\\n   - ASSIGNING: Group is computing target assignments\\n   - RECONCILING: Members are reconciling to target assignments\\n   - STABLE: All members reconciled\\n   - DEAD: Group being deleted\\n\\n   State transitions are computed in maybeUpdateGroupState() method based on:\\n   - Members list emptiness\\n   - Comparison of groupEpoch vs targetAssignmentEpoch\\n   - Whether members are reconciled to target assignment\\n\\n2. **CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java** - Encapsulates the reconciliation state machine that determines member states during ASSIGNING and RECONCILING phases\\n\\n3. **MemberState.java** (modern) - Defines individual member states:\\n   - STABLE: Member fully reconciled\\n   - UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS: Member must revoke partitions\\n   - UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS: Member waiting for partitions from other owners\\n   - UNKNOWN: Unknown state\\n\\n4. **ConsumerGroupMember.java** - Individual member implementation\\n\\n## Share and Streams Group State Machines\\n\\nSimilar state machines exist for:\\n- **ShareGroup.java** with states: EMPTY, STABLE, DEAD, UNKNOWN\\n- **StreamsGroup.java** with member-based reconciliation\\n\\n## Request Handling and Transitions\\n\\nThe primary entry points for state transitions are:\\n\\n1. **GroupMetadataManager.java** - Central coordinator containing:\\n   - classicGroupJoin() - Handles JoinGroup requests\\n   - classicGroupSync() - Handles SyncGroup requests\\n   - consumerGroupHeartbeat() - Handles heartbeat for modern groups\\n   - Supporting methods: classicGroupJoinToClassicGroup(), classicGroupJoinNewMember(), classicGroupJoinExistingMember(), classicGroupSyncToClassicGroup()\\n\\n2. **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** - Delegates to GroupMetadataManager:\\n   - classicGroupJoin() - Routes join requests\\n   - classicGroupSync() - Routes sync requests\\n\\n3. **GroupCoordinatorService.java** - API layer:\\n   - joinGroup() - Exposes JoinGroup API\\n   - syncGroup() - Exposes SyncGroup API\\n\\n## State Transition Flow\\n\\nFor classic groups, the flow is:\\n1. Member sends JoinGroup -> moves to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n2. After timeout or all members joined -> moves to COMPLETING_REBALANCE\\n3. Leader sends SyncGroup with assignments -> moves to STABLE\\n4. Any member failure or new join -> moves back to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n\\nFor modern consumer groups:\\n1. First member join -> ASSIGNING\\n2. Compute target assignments -> stays ASSIGNING until assignments available\\n3. Members reconcile -> RECONCILING\\n4. All members reconciled -> STABLE\\n\\nThe state machine is driven by records persisted in __consumer_offsets topics, making it durable and recoverable.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1619,"cache_read_input_tokens":60152,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1619},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"2494955c-3c82-4209-9091-37fbe4eb92ec","uuid":"5433b2fc-3e69-4350-9c6c-eee209864368"}
